####################### Meta Data Part #############################
	Column Name	Data Type	Description	Label	Validation Text	Unit
1	EXPEDITION	Numeric	expedition code	#	expedition code, required key field between 1 and 9999	#
2	SITE	Numeric	site, number between 1 and 9999	Site	site, required key field between 1 and 9999	#
3	HOLE	text	hole identifier, A-Z	Hole	hole, required key field '[A-Z]'	#
4	CORE	Numeric	core identifier	Core	core identifier, required field, number between 1 and 9999	#
5	SECTION	Numeric	section number	Section	section number >=0	#
6	SECTION_ID	Numeric	section identifier,	Section	section Identifier, required field #	#
7	SECTION_UNIT	Integer	currrent section-unit	Lithology	# #	#
8	TOP_INTERVAL	Double	distance from top of  section-unit to top of section	Distance To Top Of Section	real value >=0.0	cm
9	BOTTOM_INTERVAL	Double	distance from top of  section-unit to top of section	Bottom To Top Of Section	# #	cm
10	TOP_DEPTH	Double	calculated top depth of section-unit	Calculated Top Depth (mbsf)	real value >=0.0	mbsf
11	TOP_DEPTH_MCD	Double	calculated top depth of section-unit	Calculated Top Depth (mcd)	real value >=0.0	mcd
12	UNIT_CLASS	Text	lithological class of section-unit	Unit Class	text string of maximum 30 characters #	#
13	UNIT_TYPE	Text	lithological type of section-unit	Unit Type	text string of maximum 255 characters #	#
14	UNIT_DESC4	Text	structural comments	Structures	text string of maximum 255 characters #	#
15	TEXTURES	Text	optional description of textures	Textures	text string of maximum 255 characters #	#
16	CONTACT_TOP	Text	top contact type of the current section-unit	Top Contact	text string of maximum 30 characters #	#
17	CONTACT_BOTTOM	Text	bottom contact type of the current section-unit	Bottom Contact	text string of maximum 30 characters #	#
18	VEIN_INTENSITY	Double	vein intensity	vein intensity	real values #	#
19	ALTERATION	Text	grade of alteration	Alteration	required text string of max. 255 characters #	#
20	REMARKS1	Memo	#	Veins Intensity Comments	unlimited text string #	#
21	REMARKS2	Memo	#	Structural Intensity Comments	unlimited text string #	#
22	REMARKS4	Memo	#	Rock Type Comments	# #	#
23	REMARKS5	Memo	#	Alteration Intensity Comments	# #	#
24	ANALYST1	Text	initials of data operator	Geologist1	required text string of max. 5 characters #	#
25	ANALYST2	Text	initials of data operator	Geologist2	required text string of max. 5 characters #	#
26	ANALYST3	Text	initials of data operator	Geologist3	required text string of max. 5 characters #	#
27	GRAINSIZE	Text	optional description of grainsize	Grainsize	text string of maximum 30 characters #	#
28	GRAINSIZE2	Text	optional description of grainsize	Grainsize 2	text string of maximum 30 characters #	#
29	UNIT_DESC5	Text	vein feature comments	Vein Features	text string of maximum 255 characters #	#
30	UNIT_DESC3	Text	alteration comments	Alteration	text string of maximum 255 characters #	#
31	DISCONTINUITIES	Text	optional description of discontinuities	Discontinuities	text string of maximum 30 characters #	#
